020943,003568:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
020944,003569: 
020945,003570:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
020946,003571:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
020947,003572:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
020948,003573:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
020949,003574: 
020950,003575:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020951,003576:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
020952,003577:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
020953,003578:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
020954,003579:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020955,003580:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
020956,003581:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
020957,003582: 
020958,003583: 
020959,003584:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
020960,003585:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
020961,003586:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
020962,003587:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
020963,003588:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
020964,003589: 
020965,003590: 
020966,003591:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
020967,003592:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020968,003593:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
020969,003594:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020970,003595:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020971,003596: 
020972,003597: 
020973,003598:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
020974,003599:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
020975,003600:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
020976,003601: 
020977,003602: 
020978,003603:                                                                                                  #  .
020979,003604: 
020980,003605: 
020981,003606:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
020982,003607:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
020983,003608:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
020984,003609:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
020985,003610: 
020986,003611: 
020987,003612:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020988,003613:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
020989,003614:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
020990,003615:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
020991,003616:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
020992,003617:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 477 

020994,003619:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020995,003620: 
020996,003621:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
020997,003622:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
020998,003623:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
020999,003624:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
021000,003625:    4443           10604                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
021001,003626:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
021002,003627: 
021003,003628:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
021004,003629:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
021005,003630: 
021006,003631: 04,2604                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
021007,003632: 04,2604                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021008,003633: 04,2604           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
021009,003634: 04,2605           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
021010,003635: 04,2606           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
021011,003636: 04,2607           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
021012,003637: 04,2610           30001                           CA       L                                     
021013,003638: 04,2611           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
021014,003639: 04,2612           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
021015,003640: 
021016,003641: 
021017,003642:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
021018,003643:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021019,003644:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021020,003645:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021021,003646:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
021022,003647: 
021023,003648:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
021024,003649:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021025,003650:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
021026,003651:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
021027,003652:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
021028,003653:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
021029,003654:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
021030,003655:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
021031,003656:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
021032,003657:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
021033,003658:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
021034,003659:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
021035,003660:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
021036,003661: 
021037,003662: 
021038,003663:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
021039,003664:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
021040,003665:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
021041,003666:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
021042,003667:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
021043,003668:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

Page 478 

021045,003670:    4462           00004                           INHINT                                         
021046,003671:    4463           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
021047,003672:    4464           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
021048,003673:    4465           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
021049,003674:    4466           04470                           TC       +2                                    
021050,003675:    4467           04473                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
021051,003676:    4470           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  
021052,003677:    4471           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
021053,003678:    4472           05137                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
021054,003679:    4473           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
021055,003680:    4474           44747                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
021056,003681:    4475           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
021057,003682:    4476           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT

021189,003814:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
021190,003815:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
021191,003816:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
021192,003817:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
021193,003818:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
021194,003819:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
021195,003820:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
